#Plays, never before printed written by the ... Princesse the Duchess of Newcastle. Plays. Selections. 1668#

##Newcastle, Margaret Cavendish, Duchess of, 1624?-1674.##

likeness of Margaret Cavendish, Duchess of NewcastleHere on this Figure Cast a Glance,But so as if iPLAYS, Never before Printed.WRITTEN By the Thrice Noble, Illustrious, and Excellent PRINCESSE, THE D
1. TO THE READERS.
